<IMG SRC="g175220g0430121144924.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ON Semiconductor Reports First Quarter 2021 Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>PHOENIX, Ariz. &#150; May</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;3, 2021 &#150;</B> ON Semiconductor Corporation (Nasdaq: ON) today announced results for the
first quarter of 2021 with following highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP diluted earnings per share of $0.20 as compared to $(0.03) in the quarter a year ago </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

quarter a year ago </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

points quarter-over-quarter and 370 basis points year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

year ago </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record automotive revenue of $515&nbsp;million increased 5&nbsp;percent quarter-over-quarter
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We delivered strong results driven by disciplined execution in a strong demand environment across our focus <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets.</FONT> Our gross margin initiatives are beginning to show early results with first quarter gross margin expanding by 80 basis points quarter-over-quarter. We remain confident in our ability to further expand
our margins as we continue to make structural changes to the business,&#148; said Hassane El-Khoury, president and CEO of ON Semiconductor. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;The
momentum in our strategic automotive and industrial <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets</FONT> is accelerating. During the first quarter, we secured key platform design wins for our Silicon Carbide and Silicon based power products, further
solidifying our market leadership in vehicle electrification.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Selected financial results for the quarter are shown below with comparable

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Diluted shares outstanding can vary as a result of, among other things, the actual exercise of options or
vesting of restricted stock units, the incremental dilutive shares from the Company&#146;s convertible senior subordinated notes, and the repurchase or the issuance of stock or convertible notes or the sale of treasury shares. In periods when the
quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $20.72, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income per share include the anti-dilutive impact of the
Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 1.625% convertible notes. At an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% convertible notes. In
periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes, the dilutive impact of the warrants issued concurrently with such notes is included in the diluted shares outstanding. Both GAAP and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share counts are based on the Company&#146;s stock price as of April&nbsp;2, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:14pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

fair market value <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">step-up;</FONT> purchased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-process</FONT> research and development expenses; restructuring, asset impairments and other, net; goodwill impairment charges; gains
and losses on debt prepayment; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> interest expense; actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits; and certain other special items, as necessary. These special items are out of our
control and could change significantly from period to period. As a result, we are not able to reasonably estimate and separately present the individual impact or probable significance of these special items, and we are similarly unable to provide a
reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The reconciliation that is unavailable would include a forward-looking income statement, balance sheet and statement of cash flows in accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;For
this reason, we use a projected range of the aggregate amount of special items in order to calculate our projected <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expense outlook. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We believe these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures provide important supplemental
information to investors. We use these measures, together with GAAP measures, for internal managerial purposes and as a means to evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons.
However, we do not, and you should not, rely on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures alone as measures of our performance. We believe that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures reflect an
additional way of viewing aspects of our operations that, when taken together with GAAP results and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures that we also provide in our releases, provide a more complete understanding of factors
and trends affecting our business. Because <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial measures with other companies&#146;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, even if they have similar names. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>TELECONFERENCE

provide the Conference ID Number &#150; which is 5398970. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About ON Semiconductor </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">ON Semiconductor (Nasdaq: ON) is driving energy efficient electronics innovations that help make the world greener, safer, inclusive and
connected. The company has transformed into our customers&#146; supplier of choice for power, analog, sensor and connectivity solutions. The company&#146;s superior products help engineers solve their most unique design challenges in automotive,
industrial, cloud power, and Internet of Things (IoT) applications. For more information, visit http://www.onsemi.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"># # # </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Tax impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> special items
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(a-f)</FONT> is calculated using the federal statutory rate of 21% for all periods presented. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">The Company simplified its corporate structure by repatriating the economic rights of its <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> intellectual property to the United States via domestication of certain foreign subsidiaries (the &#147;Domestication&#148;) during 2020. The Domestication resulted in a benefit from recognizing certain
deferred tax assets, net of deferred tax liabilities, of $62.9&nbsp;million for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2020. Additionally, the Domestication caused the Company to reassess the full valuation allowance recorded against its U.S. state
deferred tax assets. As a result, the Company also released approximately $49.5&nbsp;million of its valuation allowance recorded against its U.S. state deferred tax assets during the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2020. Of the total
$112.4&nbsp;million described above, $110.3&nbsp;million and $2.1&nbsp;million were recorded during the third and fourth quarters of 2020, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">The income tax adjustment primarily represents the use of the net operating loss, <FONT

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the consolidated financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, ON Semiconductor uses
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">certain&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> which are adjusted from the most directly comparable GAAP measures to exclude items related to the amortization of intangible assets, amortization of acquisition-related
intangibles, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;inventory</FONT> valuation adjustments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">purchased&nbsp;in-process&nbsp;research</FONT> and
development expenses, restructuring, asset impairments and other, net, goodwill impairment charges, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension
plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, tax impact of these items and certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, as necessary. Management does not consider the effects
of these items in evaluating the core operational activities of ON Semiconductor. Management uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> internally to make strategic decisions, forecast future results and evaluate
ON Semiconductor&#146;s current performance. In addition, the Company believes that most analysts covering ON Semiconductor use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> to evaluate ON Semiconductor&#146;s performance.
Given management&#146;s and other relevant use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> ON Semiconductor believes these measures are important to investors in understanding ON Semiconductor&#146;s current and
future operating results as seen through the eyes of management. In addition, management believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are useful to investors in enabling them to better assess changes in ON
Semiconductor&#146;s core business across different time periods. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">These&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are not prepared in accordance with, and should not be considered alternatives or necessarily superior to,
GAAP financial data and may be different <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">from&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> used by other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Because&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures are not standardized, it
may not be possible to compare these financial measures with other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">companies&#146;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures, even if they have similar names. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:0%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Adjusted EBITDA </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Adjusted EBITDA is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure that represents net income before interest expense,
interest income, provision for income taxes, depreciation and amortization expense and special items. We use the adjusted EBITDA measure for internal managerial evaluation purposes, as a means to evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons and as a performance metric for the vesting and release of certain of our performance-based equity awards. SEC Regulation G and other federal securities laws regulate the use of
financial measures that are not prepared in accordance with GAAP. We believe this measure provides important supplemental information to investors. However, we do not, and you should not, rely on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
financial measures alone as measures of our performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Revenue </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue allows management to evaluate, among other things, the revenue from the
Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent of special items. In addition, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue is an important component of management&#146;s
internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future
results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of ON
Semiconductor&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Gross</FONT> Profit and Gross Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> profit and gross margin allows management to evaluate, among other
things, the gross margin and gross profit of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally
speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up</FONT> and the impact from the change in revenue recognition on distributor sales. In addition, it is an important component of
management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and
forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of revenue
of ON Semiconductor&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Operating</FONT> Income and&nbsp;Operating Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> income and operating margin allows management to evaluate,
among other things, the operating margin and operating income of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT>
including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> the impact from the change in revenue recognition on distributor sales,&nbsp;amortization and impairments of
intangible assets, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, restructuring charges and certain other special items as necessary. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and
incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NON-GAAP MEASURES (Continued) </B></P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable
investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of ON Semiconductor&#146;s core businesses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Net</FONT> Income Attributable to ON Semiconductor and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
Diluted Earnings Per Share </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income attributable to ON
Semiconductor and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share allows management to evaluate the operating results of ON Semiconductor&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a
consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally, the amortization and impairments of intangible assets, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> the impact from the change in revenue recognition on distributor sales, restructuring, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT>
expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, tax indemnification by third parties, tax impact of these items and other
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain other special items, as necessary. In addition, these items are important components of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process, as
they are used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, setting targets and forecasting future results. Management presents
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures to enable investors and analysts to understand the results of operations of ON Semiconductor&#146;s core businesses and, to the extent comparable, to compare our
results of operations on a more consistent basis against those of other companies in our industry. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Free Cash Flow </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of free cash flow allows management to evaluate, among other things, the ability of the Company to make interest or principal payments
on its debt. Free cash flow is defined as the difference between cash flow from operating activities and capital expenditures disclosed under investing activities in the consolidated statement of cash flows. Free cash flow is not an alternate to
cash flow from operating activities as a measure of liquidity. It is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results
of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to
evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of ON Semiconductor&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Share Count </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted
share count allows management to evaluate, among other things, the potential dilution due to the outstanding stock options and restricted stock units excluding the dilution from the convertible notes that is covered by hedging activity up to a
certain threshold. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $18.50, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge
transactions issued concurrently with the 1.00% convertible notes. As such, at an average stock price per share between $18.50 and $25.96, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.00% convertible notes. In periods when
the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $20.72, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with
the 1.625% convertible notes. As such, at an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% convertible notes. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>
